            <comment><![CDATA[GC-44636]]></comment>
            <expr><![CDATA[if (Strcmp(SECURITY_TYP, "SPOT"))
	if (Strcmp(INVERSE_QUOTED, "Y"))
		return StoreString("BASE CURR", Translate(BloombergETT, false, "BB_CURRENCY_CODE", CRNCY));
	else
		return StoreString("BASE CURR", "USD");
else if (Strcmp(SECURITY_TYP, "CROSS"))
	if (OneHasValue(Translate(BloombergETT, false, "BB_CURRENCY_CODE", SubString(NAME, 1, 3))))
		return StoreString("BASE CURR", Translate(BloombergETT, false, "BB_CURRENCY_CODE", SubString(NAME, 1, 3)));
	else if (Strcmp(SubString(NAME, 1, 3), "TFX") && OneHasValue(Translate(BloombergETT, false, "BB_CURRENCY_CODE", StrLeftCut(StrWord(NAME, "/", 1), 3))))
		return StoreString("BASE CURR", Translate(BloombergETT, false, "BB_CURRENCY_CODE", StrLeftCut(StrWord(NAME, "/", 1), 3)));

              <expr><![CDATA[if (Strcmp(
		Translate(Config_Options, true, "OrigSrcOrRedistAsPricesource",
				"Bloomberg_DL_Currencies"), "REDISTRIBUTOR"))
	return "BB";
else if (Strcmp(
		Translate(Config_Options, true, "OrigSrcOrRedistAsPricesource",
				"Bloomberg_DL_Currencies"), "PRICESOURCE"))
	if (OneHasValue(PRICING_SOURCE))
		return PRICING_SOURCE;
	else
		return "Not Available";
else if (!StrContainsOneOf(
		Translate(Config_Options, true, "OrigSrcOrRedistAsPricesource",
				"Bloomberg_DL_Currencies"), "PRICESOURCE", "REDISTRIBUTOR")
		|| !OneHasValue(Translate(Config_Options, true,
				"OrigSrcOrRedistAsPricesource", "Bloomberg_DL_Currencies")))
	return ThrowMapError(
			Strcat(Translate(Config_Options, true,
					"OrigSrcOrRedistAsPricesource", "Bloomberg_DL_Currencies"),
					Strcat("--",
							"Wrong value in Config_Option.xml against OrigSrcOrRedistAsPricesource. It is other than permitted value PRICESOURCE and REDISTRIBUTOR used in Config_option.xml")),
			"");
else
	return "";]]></expr>
